date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

agda: true
---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

{: .references }

  - https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
  - https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="438" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="442" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="450" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="462" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="466" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="471" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="478" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="493" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#501" class="Function">_</a> <a id="503" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="505" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="509" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="782" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="789" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#789" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="799" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="808" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="874" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="940" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1843" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1901" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1917" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1924" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1934" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1942" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1954" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1957" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1962" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1964" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1967" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1971" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="1984" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1924" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1986" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2329" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2336" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>

  <a id="2416" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2428" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2434" class="Keyword">field</a>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3082" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3087" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3092" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3094" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3100" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3390" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3405" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3413" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3420" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3424" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3424" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3429" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3433" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3438" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3438" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3442" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3447" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3451" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3469" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3586" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3586" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3591" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3593" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3595" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3608" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3612" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

#### Instance Searh

### Identity Type

Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6340" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6343" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6348" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6351" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6353" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6343" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6362" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6364" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6365" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6351" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6380" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6485" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="6491" class="Number">30</a> <a id="6494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="6503" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6527" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

[Here]({% link 2018-07-05-pathovers %}) we discuss more about Pathovers and
equivalent types.

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7296" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7303" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7303" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7324" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7324" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7326" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7328" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7329" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7333" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7338" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7324" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7340" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7342" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7484" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

<a id="7848" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7853" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7303" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8152" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8152" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8156" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8158" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8160" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8160" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8161" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8163" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8164" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8164" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8166" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8168" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8173" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8160" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8174" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8177" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8178" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8180" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8180" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8182" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8184" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8164" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8185" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8189" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8193" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8196" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8180" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8200" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8202" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8180" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8152" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8213" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5213" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8219" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8220" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8222" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5213" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8219" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

## Properties on the groupoid

<a id="9933" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9938" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9038" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

                <a id="14305" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14307" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14308" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14308" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14310" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14312" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14244" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14246" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14318" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14320" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14322" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14323" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14323" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14325" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14254" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14244" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14331" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14333" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14272" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14244" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14336" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14793" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14800" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14800" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14809" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14810" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14810" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14813" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14813" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14815" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14817" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14818" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14818" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14820" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14822" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14827" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14810" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14829" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14831" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14832" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14832" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14836" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14818" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14838" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14840" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14845" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14813" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14847" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14849" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14857" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14935" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14975" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14984" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14986" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14987" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14987" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14989" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14989" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14991" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14993" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14995" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14995" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14997" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14999" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14818" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15000" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15002" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14832" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15006" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14995" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15007" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15010" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15012" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14810" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15021" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15023" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14813" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15025" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14975" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15038" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15040" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15042" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15044" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15045" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15045" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15047" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15049" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14818" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15050" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15052" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15054" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15056" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15045" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15058" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15061" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15040" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15063" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15045" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="15068" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15068" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="15072" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15074" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15075" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15075" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15077" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15077" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15081" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15083" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15083" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14818" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15088" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15090" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15092" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14832" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15094" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15083" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15095" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15098" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15100" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15105" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14810" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15109" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14813" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15113" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15117" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15119" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15068" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15121" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15121" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15123" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15125" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14975" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15117" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15121" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="15141" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.h-refl"></a><a id="15182" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15182" class="Function">h-refl</a> <a id="15189" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15192" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15192" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15194" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15196" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15197" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15197" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15201" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14818" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15202" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15204" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15206" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14832" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15197" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15209" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15211" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15192" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15215" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15068" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15217" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15192" class="Bound">f</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

A particular case of naturality on the identity function.

## Fibers

## Equivalence

    <a id="18422" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18490" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18555" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18572" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18572" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18586" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18586" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18588" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18590" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18385" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18592" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18399" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18595" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18597" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18599" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18377" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18608" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18610" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18380" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18612" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18666" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18737" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22089" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="22096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22096" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22113" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22114" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22117" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22119" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22121" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22122" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22124" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22131" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22114" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22133" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22135" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22136" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22138" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22145" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22117" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22147" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22149" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22158" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22225" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22271" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22271" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22289" <a id="23003" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23008" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22096" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23274" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23281" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23281" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23299" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23300" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23300" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23301" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23303" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23312" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23383" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23421" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23429" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23430" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23434" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23439" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23300" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23440" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23442" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23449" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23300" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="23453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23421" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23459" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23459" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23461" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23464" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23464" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23466" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23466" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="23468" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23470" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23459" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23471" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23473" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23475" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23476" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23464" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23478" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23481" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23466" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2901" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="23486" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1675" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="23488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23489" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23464" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23491" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23466" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23495" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23500" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="23565" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>

<a id="23986" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23281" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24221" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24228" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24241" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24250" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24319" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24341" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24343" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24345" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24345" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24346" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24350" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24350" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24354" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24359" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24345" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24360" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24362" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24345" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24380" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24382" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24384" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24386" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24388" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24392" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24380" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24393" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24395" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24386" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24388" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24403" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24408" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24443" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24443" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24451" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24453" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24454" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24456" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24458" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24464" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24453" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24470" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24443" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24480" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24481" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24481" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24482" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24484" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24486" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2350" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24489" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24481" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24495" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24497" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24508" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24574" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24592" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24592" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24601" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24603" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24603" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24606" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24606" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24608" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24612" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24613" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24613" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24617" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24622" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24603" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24624" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24626" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24628" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24629" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24631" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24613" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24635" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24637" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24642" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24606" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24644" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24655" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24657" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24659" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24659" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24661" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24663" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24613" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24664" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24666" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24668" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24676" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24629" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24678" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24659" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24679" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24682" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24684" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24691" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24693" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24693" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24695" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24697" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24613" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24698" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24700" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24702" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24629" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24704" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24693" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24705" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24592" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24716" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24722" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24724" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24724" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24726" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24728" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20419" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24735" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24737" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24737" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24739" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24741" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24716" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24747" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24737" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24750" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24722" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24752" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24737" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24753" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24755" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24756" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24724" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24758" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24737" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24759" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24764" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24822" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24822" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24836" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24838" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24838" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24841" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24841" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24843" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24845" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24847" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24848" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24848" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24850" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24852" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24857" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24838" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24859" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24861" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24863" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24864" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24864" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24866" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24868" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24873" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24841" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24875" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24891" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24893" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24900" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24848" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24902" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24904" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24911" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24864" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24913" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24915" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24848" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24925" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2726" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24927" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24864" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24928" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24992" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24228" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25205" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25212" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25212" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25217" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25226" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25297" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>
  <a id="Sets.isSet"></a><a id="25313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25313" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25321" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="25323" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25323" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="25324" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="25327" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25328" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25328" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25330" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="25337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25323" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="25338" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25340" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="25347" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25323" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="25351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25313" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25357" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25359" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25362" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25362" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25364" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="25366" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25357" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25369" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24334" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="25380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25362" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="25386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25364" class="Bound">y</a><a id="25387" class="Symbol">)</a>

             <a id="25573" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25313" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25581" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25531" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25583" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25585" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25313" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25591" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25547" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25593" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25595" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25313" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25601" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25531" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25604" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2726" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="25606" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25547" class="Bound">B</a><a id="25607" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="25912" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25212" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28180" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28185" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27398" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28429" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28436" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28436" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28449" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28450" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28453" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28455" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28457" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28458" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28458" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28460" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28462" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28469" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28471" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28472" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28472" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28476" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28481" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28453" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28483" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28485" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28494" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28525" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28532" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28539" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28543" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28458" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28545" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28547" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28472" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28548" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28550" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28552" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28558" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28561" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28563" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28453" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28565" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28567" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="31107" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="31112" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28436" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31286" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31293" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31307" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31308" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31308" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31311" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31311" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31313" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31315" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31316" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31316" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31318" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31308" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31327" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31329" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31330" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31330" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31332" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31311" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31341" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31343" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="34039" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

     <a id="35503" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2444" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35508" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35116" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35515" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35430" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35516" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4058" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35520" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2444" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35524" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35430" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7641" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35534" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20419" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35541" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19688" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35558" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35430" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35559" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35561" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7641" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3586" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35574" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7740" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35575" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35578" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34324" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35782" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="35789" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35789" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="35800" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="36586" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="36591" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35851" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="36607" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Somme lemmas about Univelance

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="36685" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36688" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36727" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36788" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36837" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36856" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36871" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36936" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36989" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="37007" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37018" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="37021" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="37093" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37118" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37214" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37235" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37250" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37357" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37462" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37541" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37617" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37700" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37723" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37734" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37749" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37835" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37864" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37883" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37971" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="38081" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38169" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38212" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38228" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38231" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38265" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38345" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38365" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38380" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38450" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38515" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38564" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38582" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="38596" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
